
-- made by 1ndrew
function sandbox(var,func)
	local env = getfenv(func)
	local newenv = setmetatable({},{
		__index = function(self,k)
			if k=="script" then
				return var
			else
				return env[k]
			end
		end,
	})
	setfenv(func,newenv)
	return func
end

Script16.Name = "WeldScript"
Script16.Parent = Model1
Script16.Disabled = true
table.insert(cors,sandbox(Script16,function()
local BrickTable = {}

function RecursiveGeneric(Parent, Func, ClassLimit)
 for _, Child in pairs(Parent:GetChildren()) do
  if not ClassLimit or Child:IsA(ClassLimit) then
   Func(Child)
  end
  RecursiveGeneric(Child, Func, ClassLimit)
 end
end

RecursiveGeneric(
 script.Parent,
 function(Brick) table.insert(BrickTable, Brick) end,
 "BasePart"
)

local Base = BrickTable[1]
table.remove(BrickTable, 1)

for _, Part in pairs(BrickTable) do
 local Weld = Instance.new("Weld")

Script350.Name = "WeldScript"
Script350.Parent = Model336
Script350.Disabled = true
table.insert(cors,sandbox(Script350,function()
local BrickTable = {}

function RecursiveGeneric(Parent, Func, ClassLimit)
 for _, Child in pairs(Parent:GetChildren()) do
  if not ClassLimit or Child:IsA(ClassLimit) then
   Func(Child)
  end
  RecursiveGeneric(Child, Func, ClassLimit)
 end
end

RecursiveGeneric(
 script.Parent,
 function(Brick) table.insert(BrickTable, Brick) end,
 "BasePart"
)

local Base = BrickTable[1]
table.remove(BrickTable, 1)

for _, Part in pairs(BrickTable) do
 local Weld = Instance.new("Weld")
 Weld.Part0 = Base
 Weld.Part1 = Part
 Weld.C1 = Part.CFrame:inverse() * Base.CFrame
 Weld.Parent = Base
 Part.Anchored = false
end

Base.Anchored = false
end))
Script351.Name = "Main"
Script351.Parent = Model0
table.insert(cors,sandbox(Script351,function()
local sp = script.Parent
local mainparts = script.Parent.Body.MainParts
local seat = mainparts.VehicleSeat
local backlight = mainparts.BackLight
local frontright = mainparts.FrontRightLight
local frontleft = mainparts.FrontLeftLight


seat.Changed:connect(function()
	if seat.Throttle == -1 then
		backlight.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Bright red")
		backlight.PointLight.Enabled = true
	else backlight.BrickColor = BrickColor.new("Black")
		backlight.PointLight.Enabled = false
	end
	if seat.Steer == 0 and seat.Throttle == 0 then
		seat.EngineOn:Stop()
	else
		seat.EngineOn:Play()
	end
end)

seat.ChildAdded:connect(function(cha)
	if cha.Name ~= "SeatWeld" then return end
	local player = game.Players:GetPlayerFromCharacter(cha.Part1.Parent);
	if player then
		CopyA = script.WarthogGui:Clone()
		CopyA.Parent = player:FindFirstChild("PlayerGui")
		Link = Instance.new("ObjectValue", CopyA.GuiScript)
		Link.Value = seat
		Link.Name = "ObjectLink"
		CopyA.GuiScript.Disabled = false
	end
	player.Character.Humanoid.Changed:connect(function()
		if not (player and player.Character and player.Character.Humanoid.Sit) then
			CopyA:Destroy()
			if player.Character ~= nil then
				if player.Character.Torso:FindFirstChild("BodyGyro") ~= nil then
					player.Character.Torso:FindFirstChild("BodyGyro"):Destroy()
				end
			end
		end
	end)
end)
end))

function RecursiveGeneric(Parent, Func, ClassLimit)

  if not ClassLimit or Child:IsA(ClassLimit) then
   Func(Child)
  end
  RecursiveGeneric(Child, Func, ClassLimit)
 end
end

RecursiveGeneric(
 script.Parent,
 function(Brick) table.insert(BrickTable, Brick) end,
 "BasePart"
)

local Base = BrickTable[1]
table.remove(BrickTable, 1)

for _, Part in pairs(BrickTable) do
 local Weld = Instance.new("Weld")
 Weld.Part0 = Base
 Weld.Part1 = Part
 Weld.C1 = Part.CFrame:inverse() * Base.CFrame
 Weld.Parent = Base
 Part.Anchored = false
end

Base.Anchored = false
end))
IntValue405.Name = "HealthValue"
IntValue405.Parent = Model0
IntValue405.Value = 5000
Script406.Parent = IntValue405
table.insert(cors,sandbox(Script406,function()
local Smoke = script.Parent.Parent.Body.Parts.EngineSmoke.Smoke
local Fire = script.Parent.Parent.Body.Parts.EngineSmoke.Fire
local ExplosionEffect = false

local Seat = script.Parent.Parent.Body.MainParts.Seat

local Stage1Cap = 1900
local Stage2Cap = 1500
local Stage3Cap = 1

script.Parent.Changed:connect(function(Change)
	if Change <= Stage1Cap then
		Smoke.Enabled = true
	elseif Change > Stage1Cap then
		Smoke.Enabled = false
	end
	if Change <= Stage2Cap then
		Fire.Enabled = true
	elseif Change > Stage2Cap then
		Fire.Enabled = false
	end
	if Change <= Stage3Cap then
		ExplosionEffect = true
	elseif Change > Stage3Cap then
		ExplosionEffect = false
	end
	if Change <= 0 then
		Instance.new("Explosion", Seat).Position = Seat.Position
		Instance.new("Explosion", Seat).BlastRadius = 5
		Instance.new("Explosion", Seat).BlastPressure = 5
		wait(5)
		if script.Parent.Parent ~= nil then
			script.Parent.Parent:Destroy()
		end
	end
end)

while wait(.1) do
	local Part = script.Parent.Parent.Body.Parts.EngineSmoke
	if ExplosionEffect == true then
		local FakeExplosion = Instance.new("Explosion", Part)
		FakeExplosion.Position = Part.Position
		FakeExplosion.BlastRadius = 0
		FakeExplosion.BlastPressure = 0
	else end
end
end))
for i,v in pairs(mas:GetChildren()) do
	v.Parent = workspace
	pcall(function() v:MakeJoints() end)
end
mas:Destroy()
for i,v in pairs(cors) do
	spawn(function()
		pcall(v)
	end)
end
Model0:MakeJoints()
Model0:MoveTo(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head.Position)
